< text>
I got the number 1, which is a large beef soup with beef balls, soft tendons, rare beef that is cooking in the boiling hot broth with rice noodles. The place is pretty big and can pretty much sit where you want. The broth was delicious and flavorful. The employees here were nice, didn't really talk much, but I'm ok with that. I had a Thai tea to go with my drink it was yummy. I would go again.< /text>

< Review>
Pho the Gioi Inc. is not my go-to pho restaurant, but the service is quick, food portions are decent and there is no minimum payment for debit card/credit card.

Their various broths are OK. I've had better. I have to season my pho to the fullest in order for it not to be bland.

There is a parking lot, so that's a plus. Wait time is short ~5 minutes or less. Servers are accommodating to small or large groups.<//Review>

<user_name>Amir S< /user_name>< text>
This little pho shop is nestled up higher in the mountains and is hidden from people who just stay close to the main streets. The first thing that I noticed is that all of the beef was higher quality than other places I've tried. The texture of the meatballs was smoother and more consistent. The noodles were more chewy. The broth was flavorful, and I only added a little bit of sauce to introduce spiciness and tanginess. The beansprouts and basil were very fresh. I ate there in the later evening hours of a weekday, around 8pm, and the atmosphere was clean and relatively quiet, and the staff was very attentive and the food arrived within minutes of ordering. The price is also a bit more affordable.< /text>

<user_id>114212414689351266817<//user_id><username>David Hume< /username><Date>1446948271609</Date>< rate>
1< /rate>
< Text>
A literal 1 star pho place. Maybe 2 stars on a really really really good day. I have tried it twice just in case, just to make sure, but it remains a 1 star pho place and there is no hope for it.

Broth is a mix of beef-grease and MSG.
Meat is barely recognizable hacked brown lumps.
Noodles are barely cooked.

Interior is basically the same as any hole in the wall pho place, but I have reviewed probably about a hundred by now. Every single one was better. Pho the Gioi is the worst pho I have had from anywhere at any time.

It is actually better to get any JML soup, or a box of pho stock and some top ramen and just scissor cut some beef yourself-- than to eat this. If you're looking for good pho in the absolute closest area, your only option is Ben Tre for like 3 or 4 star pho. Your other option is Pho Saigon for other 1 or 2 star pho, slightly better than Pho the Gioi.< /Text>

< Text>
Brought my 69 Camaro here many times to do thousands of dollars of business 2012-2013.  They were very nice and knowledgeable.  So not sure why this happened.  I brought two carbs in, one was the original two barrel which was installed in the car and other was a four barrel Holley.  I was contemplating which to put in.  The head guy there said it was a coincidence that there was a Holley there that another customer brought in that was identical to mine but was leaking from everywhere a carb could leak.  After discussing the carbs with him I decided to leave the two barrel on the car.  He asked if I was sure and did I think I would ever use the Holley and I thought it odd he asked me a few times and also right before I left.  I said I would not, my mind was made up, I picked up the car and the Holley was put in its original box.  Well after a couple weeks I decided to try the Holley again.  I installed it and the car would not start.  I thought it was weird and kept trying to turn it over.  Finally I went to the carb and there was fuel all over the top of the engine.  I realized then the reason why he had confirmed with me more than once that I had not planned to use the carb, it was because they switched the leaky one with mine after I assured him I was not going to use it.

Be very careful if you bring parts in there.  Mark them in some way and take a pic.   I‚Äôve never been back and I‚Äôm kind of sad as I thought there was a kind of friendship.

This incident happened in 2013 and it‚Äôs bugged me for a long time.  I just had given the shop a one star rating with no explanation.  Finally decided an explanation is needed.  I hope the guy is still there and reads this and remembers.  I wasn‚Äôt angry at the time nor now I‚Äôm just disappointed and sad at the situation.  At least he‚Äôll know I was aware of what happened.< /Text>

< Review>
as a library it's ok, although for a while there was one white guy working there who seemed a bit like a bully...not sure if he's still there.. I always kind of felt like I was in "his library" rather than the community's library..BUT the REAL REASON I am taking time to make this review is related to an incident that occurred. I was at the library one day and as I was leaving a young man came up to me and said, "Excuse me, I think I hear a baby crying in the van over there..." He wanted me to help. So I walked over to the vehicle and SURE ENOUGH there was a baby inside. We couldn't see it but we could hear it. All the windows were closed & doors locked, so we went into the library together and reported it...and they made an announcement over the loudspeaker. We waited outside to see if somebody would come and eventually somebody did. What BOTHERED ME in addition to the potential danger the baby was in..was that as we gathered around to watch to make sure the baby was ok, one of the library employees tried to tell us to GO AWAY, as if it was NONE OF OUR BUSINESS if the baby is ok or  not. I backed up but did NOT LEAVE..I had to see for myself..turns out the woman worked at a daycare and this baby was one of many children she had taken to the library that day, the others were old enough to enjoy the kids program, but the infant was left in the van...apparently with no concern that it might get too hot in there. The library employee seemed to be more intent on "white washing" it. They did NOT even thank us, and seemed to be ready to let it go at that. But I CALLED the POLICE and reported it. And I am glad to say an officer came immediately...and a report was made to social services etc, ..I eventually was called as a witness in a hearing..not sure what happened in the end. Main thing we hope the baby was okay. Just wish the library had been a little more TRANSPARENT about the issue and had shown some appreciation rather than trying to cover it up. As citizens we are ALWAYS watched and being told what we are doing wrong...be it driving or parking, but never being THANKED or appreciated for moments such as this ..when we may have saved a baby's life.< /Review>

Ain't bad. This is the place to go for what I recall is the "sunrise platter" (might be what it's called. Don't hold me to it). Slices of ham, hash browns with cheese, gravy, bacon, and a couple of eggs. Super savory, and packs in the flavor. This was written during covid so I can't speak for the dine-in experience but it's a busy spot so it's not like you're going to have a quiet or luxury dining experience. There's always a lunch rush. If a hearty, savory breakfast ain't doing it for you they got wraps, burgers, wings, and sandwiches. Specialty shakes are also displayed on their menu and though a little pricey you do get what you pay for. Parking is the only real pain of deciding to eat here. Either park around back if you don't see a spot in the front or I'd walk a block or so. Trust me, I drive around the area every day for work and it's safer and easier to pick a nice parking spot than to jam in some skinny spot where you're backing into the street or pulling some fancy maneuvers.< /text>

<Time>1602180847366< /Time><Review>Hard core New Yorkers may be offended. Others may find this place quite delightful. A local eatery that is more like a dinner rather than a mom & pop joint.

The menu is vast and there is a dish for everyone including vegans, vegetarians, kids, fruitarians, dessert only, and those with no teeth. Meals range from a bagel to a full course, which includes breakfast, lunch, and dinner.

On this first time eat, I had the waffle plate and pastrami and cheese. I saw the French toast and malibu omelette. Which appeared quite appetizing. There is a variety of omelette creations that should be tried.

The waffle batter must have vanilla because it is truly flavorful. Crisp on the top and edges and soft on the outside. Not soggy. Not hard. Accurately cooked. The dish is accompanied by eggs and bacon for under $10 bucks. What is noticeable is the eggs appear to be larger in size and the waffle was delightful. Get whip cream instead of butter and syrup.

The pastrami had good flavor. Very cheesy. It also had lots of fat which became annoying to eat. Unless fat meat is your groove. However, the golden sourdough üçû and presentation of the meal was mouth-watering. I would not have the pastrami again but would try another sandwich with the grilled sourdough.

Portion size was more than adequate. I arrived@130 pm and timeliness of order was 10 minutes. Food is prepared upon order. Masha are required. Seating is limited but it is not a place to eat and hangout all day. Wheelchair accessible. Dine-in is available but you'll likely eat outside. Parking? Prepare to walk about a block. Bathroom, unisex toilet, was decent but on the verge of a scary gasoline pit stop bathroom. Prices are similar to "diner eating."</Review><gmapID>0x80d95a064f35e5c3:0xca5d6d698eeb5911<//gmapID>< username>

I moved from Colorado a year ago and I always look for good food, specially burritos. <Text>My husband and I just moved to the area and decided to try out Sunrise Deli. We have been back many times since! They have an extensive menu and cook the food to order so it is always hot and fresh. The staff are always super friendly (except for the one young girl who couldn't hear us because she didn't want to take her headphones out haha!). The majority of the time, our food is delicious and the prices are great. I do have to check before we leave each time though because 1) they always leave on the tomato when I ask for none and 2) the bacon is never crispy even though we ask. These are such minor details though. Overall, I am very happy with our experiences here. I would not come here if you're in a rush, or at least call ahead. They do cook your food when you order so it takes about 10-15 minutes to get your food. That is worth it to us! It is also about half the price of similar restaurants for what you're getting. Both my husband and I can get a full meal for under $20 and it's a lot of food! Even the kids meals are good sized. You will get your monies worth!< /Text><Gmap_id>0x80d95a064f35e5c3:0xca5d6d698eeb5911</Gmap_id>< Pictures>
